#Coring Decisions
DEBUG_Coring_Decisions = {

DEBUG_Core_Whole_World = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 0
		modifier = { }

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
		
	}

DEBUG_Core_Owned_States = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 0
		modifier = { }

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_controlled_by = FROM NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	DEBUG_Transfer_Cores = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 0
		modifier = { }

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_owned_by = FROM } is_core_of = FROM }
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
	}

}


GEN_Empire_Manager = {

	show_hide_formables_decisions = {
        priority = 100
        visible = { always = yes }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

        complete_effect = { 
            if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag = show_formables_decisions }
                clr_country_flag = show_formables_decisions
            }
            else = {
                set_country_flag = show_formables_decisions
            }
        }
    }
	

	show_hide_integration_decisions = {
        priority = 100
        visible = { always = yes }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

        complete_effect = { 
            if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag = show_integration_decisions }
                clr_country_flag = show_integration_decisions
            }
            else = {
                set_country_flag = show_integration_decisions
            }
        }
    }
	
	BFN_coring_states_targeted_decision = {
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
    state_target = yes
    target_root_trigger = {
    }
    target_array = controlled_states
    target_trigger = {
        FROM = {
			NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
			any_neighbor_state = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
        }
    }
	available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 9
	}
	visible = {
			has_war = no
            NOT = { has_country_flag = show_integration_decisions }
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } 
				#NOT = { has_state_flag = Coring_In_Progress } 
			}
       }
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power < 150
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				has_government = fascism
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				date < 1940.1.1
			}
		}
	modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 10 }
	days_remove = 30
    on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
    cost = 50
	
    complete_effect = {
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	FROM = { 
		#		set_state_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		#	}
		#}
	}
	remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			FROM = {
				add_core_of = ROOT
				#clr_state_flag = Coring_In_Progress
			}
	}
}

GGR_Coring_Decisions = {

	##Actual Formable
	#Greater Germanic Reich
	RON_Formable_Decision1 = {
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = fascism
				date < 1945.1.1
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
		}
		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			original_tag = GER
			NOT = { has_country_flag = show_formables_decisions }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = FORM_GGR2 }
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = GER
			NOT = { has_global_flag = FORM_GGR2 }
			#is_subject = no
			has_global_flag = FORM_GRO2
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_POL_Neutralized_tt
				OR = {
					POL = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
					POL = {
						exists = no
					}
					POL = {
						is_subject_of = GER
					}
					OR = {
						GER = {
							controls_state = 10
						}
						any_other_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_FRA_Neutralized_tt

							has_capitulated = yes
						}

							exists = no
						}

							is_subject_of = GER
						}

							NOT = { GER = { has_war_with = SOV } }
							OR = {

									owns_state = 219
								}

									is_in_faction_with = GER

								}
							}

									owns_state = 195
								}

									owns_state = 195
								}
								any_other_country = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
									owns_state = 195
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.6 }
